     в”Ӯ .env.*, !.env.example, *.pem, *.key, *.pfx, *.p12, id_rsa*, secrets/,   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ .claude/settings.local.json); create .claudeignore (same secret         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ patterns); commit .env.example                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ (placeholders only). This closes a verified gap вҖ” current .gitignore    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ violates the repo's own rule.                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3.2 Key models                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - LogEvent(source, file, line_no, timestamp{aware,UTC}, ip, user,       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ method, path, status, size, message, extra)                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - ParseFailure(file, line_no, reason) вҖ” counted + WARN-logged, never    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ raises (malformed line вү  crash).                                        в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ 3.3 Detection rules (all streaming-safe via per-IP                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ SlidingWindowCounter)                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: web-brute-force / ssh-brute-force                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: failures per IP in window вүҘ threshold                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: threshold, window_seconds, match filters                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: web-/ssh-brute-force-success                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: brute-force state + subsequent success same IP вҶ’ CRITICAL    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: threshold, window, success_statuses                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: path-traversal                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: patterns on raw and URL-decoded path (../, %2e%2e%2f, %252e) в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: patterns                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: sqli-probe                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: keyword patterns (union select, drop table, ' or 1=1, ;--) вҖ” в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ bare                                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ apostrophe (O'Brien) must NOT flag                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: patterns                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: scanner-burst                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: distinct sensitive paths w/ 403/404 per IP                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: threshold, window, statuses, probe_paths                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: rate-limit-abuse                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: 429s per IP in window                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: threshold, window, statuses                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: sudo-sensitive-command                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: COMMAND= vs sensitive patterns (/etc/shadow, .ssh/,          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ id_rsaвҖҰ);                                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ systemctl restart nginx stays benign                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: sensitive_patterns                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: ssh-invalid-user-enum                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: distinct invalid usernames per IP                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: threshold, window                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: rapid-success-after-failures                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: success вүӨ max_gap after вүҘ min_failures                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: min_failures, max_gap_seconds                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: multi-vector-correlation                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: вүҘ2 distinct rule hits, one IP, вүҘ2 sources, in window вҶ’       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ CRITICAL                                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ referencing child findings                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: min_distinct_rules, require_distinct_sources, window      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ config/rules.yaml: version, defaults.window_seconds,                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ alerts.{min_severity,sinks:[toast,email]},                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ rules[] with id/type/enabled/severity/source/<knobs>. Loader: unknown   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ type вҶ’ error listing valid                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ types; regexes compiled at load, ReDoS-reviewed (no nested quantifiers, в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ anchored), lines >8 KB                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ pre-truncated; bad YAML вҶ’ exit 2 with actionable message, never a       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ traceback.                                                              в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ 3.5 Concurrency (the "queueing/load balancer" answer)                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ In-process JobQueue(max_pending=100) (bounded вҶ’ explicit backpressure:  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ QueueFull surfaced as                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ retryable error in CLI/TUI) + WorkerPool(workers=4) daemon threads +    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ lock-guarded JobRegistry                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ (get/list/cancel вҖ” cooperative cancel flag) + graceful                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ shutdown(timeout) (sentinels + join).                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Per-job try/except вҶ’ FAILED with redacted error; worker survives (no    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ pool poisoning). Textual                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ integration strictly via app.call_from_thread. No Redis/Celery вҖ” a      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ self-contained CLI must run                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ on a fresh reviewer machine via pip install; README documents the       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ scaling seam: JobQueue is an                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ interface вҶ’ swap distributed broker (Redis/SQS), raise workers, shard   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ by file.                                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3.6 AuthN/AuthZ (roles justified: smallest realistic SOC set)           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - analyst: RUN_ANALYSIS, STOP_OWN_JOB, VIEW_FINDINGS,                   в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ Permission.X)) вҖ” TUI merely hides                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ options. Lockout: 5 consecutive failures вҶ’ 15 min (A07). Password       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ policy вүҘ12 chars mixed classes.                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ CLI auth via SLAT_USERNAME/SLAT_PASSWORD env or getpass; TUI via login  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ screen. DB at                                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ %LOCALAPPDATA%/security-log-analysis-tool/users.db (XDG on posix) вҖ”     в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ interpretation)                                                         в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ (expected <10 s), (2) each                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ job's findings match expectation, (3) shutdown(timeout=10) returns True в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ and thread count back to                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ baseline, (4) pytest-timeout hard-kills at 90 s on deadlock. Throughput в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ attached to Allure. Negative:                                           в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ successfully AND app never hangs.                                       в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ - Domain fit: log parsing/detection is text-wrangling + rules; re,      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ datetime, dataclasses and                                               в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ it natively.                                                            в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ depth, and TUI/report polish under 48h вҖ” no Textual/Pilot or            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ allure-pytest equivalents.                                              в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ worker_threads ceremony), thinner                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ security ecosystem, no headless TUI test harness of Pilot's quality.    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Scaling story is architectural, not runtime: streaming pipeline,      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ bounded queue, worker seam                                              в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ Choice: stdlib smtplib + EmailMessage, STARTTLS, creds only from .env   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Why (one line): locked decision                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Concern: Toast                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Choice: port .claude/scripts/notify-desktop.ps1 WinRT approach вҶ’        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ alerts/toast.ps1 via subprocess; try/except no-op off-Windows           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Why (one line): proven code in repo; sink must never fail the caller    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Concern: Unit/E2E/perf tests                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Choice: pytest>=8, pytest-timeout>=2.3, pytest-asyncio>=0.24            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Why (one line): timeout = "no hang" backstop                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Concern: BDD regression                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Choice: behave>=1.2.6 вҖ” real Gherkin .feature files + step              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ implementations                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Why (one line): user-mandated; steps reuse the same engine/fixture      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ builders as                                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ unit tests                                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Concern: Reporting                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Choice: allure-pytest>=2.13.5 + allure-behave>=2.13.5                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Why (one line): locked decision; both runners write the SAME            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ allure-results dir                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ вҶ’ one merged report                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Concern: SMTP mock                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Choice: aiosmtpd>=1.4.6 (dev)                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Why (one line): agentic email test, no real creds                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Concern: SARIF check                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Choice: jsonschema>=4.23 (dev)                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Why (one line): validate SARIF 2.1.0 before trusting GitHub upload      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Concern: Docker                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Choice: python:3.12-slim, single-stage, non-root                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Why (one line): pure-Python вҶ’ multi-stage buys nothing (comment in      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Dockerfile);                                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ no HEALTHCHECK (short-lived CLI, documented)                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Concern: Jenkins                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Choice: native Windows install (JDK present)                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Why (one line): fastest to demo/screenshot; Docker alternative          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ documented only                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ pyproject.toml: dependencies = ["textual>=1.0,<2", "pyyaml>=6.0.1"];    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ dev extras as above.                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3. Architecture                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3.1 Module layout (src/security_log_analysis_tool/)                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ cli.py                      # analyze | watch | tui | users             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ {add,list,remove,seed-demo} | --version                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ config.py                   # AppConfig; rules.yaml loader+validation;  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ tiny .env loader                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ models.py                   # LogEvent, ParseFailure, Finding,          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Evidence, Job, User; enums (frozen dataclasses)                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ redaction.py                # redact(text):                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ passwords/tokens/keys/emails вҖ” used by logging + ALL exports            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ logging_setup.py            # dictConfig: Rich console + rotating       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ app.log/app.jsonl + RedactionFilter                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ parsers/                    # base.py (Parser protocol, pure),          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ apache_access.py, syslog_auth.py, registry+sniffer                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ detection/                  # base.py (Rule protocol +                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ SlidingWindowCounter), brute_force.py, web_attacks.py,                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                             #   scanner.py, rate_limit.py,              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sudo_rules.py, ssh_enum.py, login_anomaly.py, registry                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ correlation/engine.py       # same-IP multi-vector across sources вҶ’     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ CRITICAL correlated finding                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ pipeline/engine.py          # AnalysisEngine: files вҶ’ events вҶ’ rules вҶ’  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ correlation вҶ’ findings; per-line fail-closed                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ pipeline/queue.py           # JobQueue(bounded) + WorkerPool +          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ JobRegistry + graceful shutdown + backpressure                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ pipeline/watch.py           # tail-follow (poll+seek, rotation-aware) вҶ’ в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ incremental engine; clean Ctrl+C                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ alerts/                     # AlertSink protocol + AlertDispatcher (the в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ app-level hook system, min-severity gate),                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                             #   email_sink.py, toast_sink.py +          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ toast.ps1                                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ auth/                       # passwords.py (scrypt), store.py (SQLite), в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ service.py (login+lockout), authz.py (Permission map)                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ export/                     # json_export.py, csv_export.py,            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sarif_export.py (SARIF 2.1.0, repo-relative URIs)                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ report/console.py           # Rich tables: findings by severity,        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ correlation callouts, summary                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ tui/app.py + tui/screens/   # login, main_menu, new_analysis, jobs,     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ findings, tool_logs                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Repo-level new files: config/rules.yaml, sample_logs/access.log +       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sample_logs/auth.log,                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ tests/{unit,e2e,perf,fixtures}/, features/*.feature +                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ features/steps/*.py +                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ features/environment.py (behave BDD regression suite),                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ .github/workflows/ci.yml, Jenkinsfile, Dockerfile, .dockerignore,       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ .env.example,                                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ .claudeignore, docs/manual-tests.md, docs/e2e-report.md.                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Commit 1 hygiene (before any feature code): append secrets floor to     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ .gitignore (.env,                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ .env.*, !.env.example, *.pem, *.key, *.pfx, *.p12, id_rsa*, secrets/,   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ .claude/settings.local.json); create .claudeignore (same secret         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ patterns); commit .env.example                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ (placeholders only). This closes a verified gap вҖ” current .gitignore    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ violates the repo's own rule.                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3.2 Key models                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - LogEvent(source, file, line_no, timestamp{aware,UTC}, ip, user,       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ method, path, status, size, message, extra)                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - ParseFailure(file, line_no, reason) вҖ” counted + WARN-logged, never    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ raises (malformed line вү  crash).                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Finding(finding_id, rule_id, severity{LOW..CRITICAL}, title,          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ description{redacted}, ip, users,                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ evidence[(file,line_no,excerpt-redacted)], first_seen, last_seen,       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ count, correlated_rule_ids)                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Job(job_id, status{QUEUED,RUNNING,DONE,FAILED,CANCELLED}, files,      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ submitted_by, timestamps, findings, error, stats)                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - User(username, password_hash, role{ADMIN,ANALYST}, failed_attempts,   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ locked_until)                                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3.3 Detection rules (all streaming-safe via per-IP                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ SlidingWindowCounter)                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: web-brute-force / ssh-brute-force                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: failures per IP in window вүҘ threshold                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: threshold, window_seconds, match filters                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: web-/ssh-brute-force-success                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: brute-force state + subsequent success same IP вҶ’ CRITICAL    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: threshold, window, success_statuses                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: path-traversal                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: patterns on raw and URL-decoded path (../, %2e%2e%2f, %252e) в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: patterns                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: sqli-probe                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: keyword patterns (union select, drop table, ' or 1=1, ;--) вҖ” в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ bare                                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ apostrophe (O'Brien) must NOT flag                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: patterns                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: scanner-burst                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: distinct sensitive paths w/ 403/404 per IP                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: threshold, window, statuses, probe_paths                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: rate-limit-abuse                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: 429s per IP in window                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: threshold, window, statuses                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: sudo-sensitive-command                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: COMMAND= vs sensitive patterns (/etc/shadow, .ssh/,          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ id_rsaвҖҰ);                                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ systemctl restart nginx stays benign                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: sensitive_patterns                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: ssh-invalid-user-enum                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: distinct invalid usernames per IP                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: threshold, window                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: rapid-success-after-failures                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: success вүӨ max_gap after вүҘ min_failures                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: min_failures, max_gap_seconds                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Rule id: multi-vector-correlation                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Mechanism: вүҘ2 distinct rule hits, one IP, вүҘ2 sources, in window вҶ’       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ CRITICAL                                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ referencing child findings                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Config knobs: min_distinct_rules, require_distinct_sources, window      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ config/rules.yaml: version, defaults.window_seconds,                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ alerts.{min_severity,sinks:[toast,email]},                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ rules[] with id/type/enabled/severity/source/<knobs>. Loader: unknown   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ type вҶ’ error listing valid                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ types; regexes compiled at load, ReDoS-reviewed (no nested quantifiers, в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ anchored), lines >8 KB                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ pre-truncated; bad YAML вҶ’ exit 2 with actionable message, never a       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ traceback.                                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3.4 Sample data (sample_logs/, committed вҖ” SARIF locations point here)  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ access.log (~120 lines) + auth.log (~80 lines), 03/Jul/2025, containing в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ exactly the assessment                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ scenarios: 10.0.0.50 web /login brute force вҶ’ 200 AND ssh               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ FailedвҶ’Accepted (the showcase                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ correlation); 203.0.113.5 admin-scan + traversal AND ssh invalid-user   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ enum (second correlation);                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ SQLi probes; O'Brien legit lookalike (negative); 429 burst; cat         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ /etc/shadow (flag) vs                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ systemctl restart nginx (don't); one malformed mid-file line; benign    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ bulk. tests/fixtures/ adds                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ per-rule known-good/known-bad slices + adversarial cases (1 MB line,    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ NUL bytes, ANSI escapes,                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ future timestamps, missing TZ).                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3.5 Concurrency (the "queueing/load balancer" answer)                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ In-process JobQueue(max_pending=100) (bounded вҶ’ explicit backpressure:  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ QueueFull surfaced as                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ retryable error in CLI/TUI) + WorkerPool(workers=4) daemon threads +    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ lock-guarded JobRegistry                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ (get/list/cancel вҖ” cooperative cancel flag) + graceful                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ shutdown(timeout) (sentinels + join).                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Per-job try/except вҶ’ FAILED with redacted error; worker survives (no    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ pool poisoning). Textual                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ integration strictly via app.call_from_thread. No Redis/Celery вҖ” a      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ self-contained CLI must run                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ on a fresh reviewer machine via pip install; README documents the       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ scaling seam: JobQueue is an                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ interface вҶ’ swap distributed broker (Redis/SQS), raise workers, shard   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ by file.                                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3.6 AuthN/AuthZ (roles justified: smallest realistic SOC set)           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - analyst: RUN_ANALYSIS, STOP_OWN_JOB, VIEW_FINDINGS,                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ VIEW_OWN_TOOL_LOGS, EXPORT_FINDINGS                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - admin: all of the above + MANAGE_USERS, MANAGE_RULES,                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ VIEW_ALL_TOOL_LOGS (all levels), STOP_ANY_JOB                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Enforcement in the service layer (authz.require(principal,              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Permission.X)) вҖ” TUI merely hides                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ options. Lockout: 5 consecutive failures вҶ’ 15 min (A07). Password       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ policy вүҘ12 chars mixed classes.                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ CLI auth via SLAT_USERNAME/SLAT_PASSWORD env or getpass; TUI via login  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ screen. DB at                                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ %LOCALAPPDATA%/security-log-analysis-tool/users.db (XDG on posix) вҖ”     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ never in repo. Dummy accounts                                           в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 6. Test strategy                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Pyramid & markers: unit вҶ’ regression (YAML BDD) вҶ’ E2E (CLI subprocess + в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Textual Pilot) вҶ’ perf.                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Markers: smoke, regression, e2e, perf, owasp. Smoke = pytest -m smoke   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ (~15 fast tests);                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ full regression = pytest (everything). Every bugfix ships a regression  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ test.                                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Gherkin BDD mechanism (behave вҖ” user-mandated): regression scenarios    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ live in real Gherkin                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ features/*.feature files (detection.feature, correlation.feature,       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ export.feature,                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ auth.feature, queue.feature) with GIVEN/WHEN/THEN scenarios, positive   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ AND negative (e.g.                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ GIVEN the app is running WHEN it receives 20 concurrent logs THEN all   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ jobs finish successfully AND                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ the app never hangs; GIVEN an analyst session WHEN they invoke an admin в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ operation THEN it is                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ denied). features/steps/*.py implement steps by reusing the same        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ engine/fixture builders as the                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ unit tests; features/environment.py handles setup/teardown. Run:        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ behave -f allure_behave.formatter:AllureFormatter -o allure-results     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ features вҖ” same                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ allure-results dir as pytest, so the merged Allure report reads as one  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ BDD living document.                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Division of labor: behave = regression BDD, pytest =                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ unit/e2e/perf/owasp. Smoke slice runs                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ both: pytest -m smoke + behave --tags=@smoke.                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ OWASP Top 10 mapping (each row вүҘ1 positive + вүҘ1 negative test, marker   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ owasp):                                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ OWASP: A01 Access Control                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Tests: full authorization matrix (confirmed in scope): every Permission в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Г— both                                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ roles, positive AND negative вҖ” analyst credentials invoking each admin  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ operation (users add/remove, VIEW_ALL_TOOL_LOGS, STOP_ANY_JOB,          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ MANAGE_RULES)                                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ via CLI and service layer вҮ’ AuthorizationError; admin succeeds; analyst в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ cannot stop another user's job; locked account rejected even with       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ correct                                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ password; enforcement proven at service layer (not just hidden UI); TUI в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ hides                                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ  admin menu for analyst                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ OWASP: A02 Crypto Failures                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Tests: scrypt hash вү  plaintext; unique salts; raw db bytes contain      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ neither                                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ dummy password                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ OWASP: A03 Injection                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Tests: admin' OR '1'='1' -- login fails, no row created; ANSI/HTML/; rm в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ -rf log                                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ line inert in console/JSON/SARIF; traversal-shaped file args confined   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ w/                                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ clean error                                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ OWASP: A05 Misconfiguration                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Tests: defaults audited: lockout on, RedactionFilter installed,         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ .env.example                                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ has no real-looking secrets, SMTP defaults to STARTTLS                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ OWASP: A07 Auth Failures                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Tests: lockout after 5 fails + unlock after window; weak password       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ rejected;                                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ hmac.compare_digest used                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ OWASP: A09 Logging Failures                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Tests: login + job lifecycle produce structured records; password never в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ appears                                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ in app.log/app.jsonl after failed login containing it                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Perf test вҖ” 20 concurrent jobs (tests/perf/test_concurrent_jobs.py,     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ @pytest.mark.perf,                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ @pytest.mark.timeout(90)): generate 20 log files (~300 lines each,      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ per-job IP offsets вҶ’                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ deterministic findings) into tmp_path; JobQueue(max_pending=32) +       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ WorkerPool(4); submit all;                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ asserts proving "no hang": (1) all 20 DONE before a 60 s soft deadline  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ (expected <10 s), (2) each                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ job's findings match expectation, (3) shutdown(timeout=10) returns True в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ and thread count back to                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ baseline, (4) pytest-timeout hard-kills at 90 s on deadlock. Throughput в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ attached to Allure. Negative:                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ job with nonexistent path вҶ’ FAILED, subsequent good job still           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ completes. BDD scenario: GIVEN app                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ running AND receives 20 concurrent logs THEN all jobs finish            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ successfully AND app never hangs.                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ README states explicitly: homework-scale by design; production =        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sustained load, larger files, more                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ workers, distributed broker behind the JobQueue seam.                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Additional performance tests (all @pytest.mark.perf, homework-scale,    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ each with a documented                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ production-scaling note):                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Streaming throughput: 100k-line synthetic access log вҶ’ assert a       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ lines/s floor (calibrated                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ locally, generous margin for CI) AND bounded memory via tracemalloc     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ peak cap вҖ” proves the                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ pipeline streams instead of materializing the file.                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Backpressure under saturation: submit 2Г— max_pending jobs вҶ’ excess    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ raise QueueFull                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ promptly (<100 ms, no blocking), all accepted jobs still complete,      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ queue drains to empty.                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Watch-mode sustained ingestion: append batches to a live-watched file в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ for ~10 s вҶ’ processing                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ lag does not grow monotonically and memory stays stable (no unbounded   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ buffering).                                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Adversarial parse-time bound (ReDoS guard): 1 MB line + pathological  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ near-miss patterns parse                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ in bounded time per line вҖ” turns the ReDoS mitigation into an asserted  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ number, not a claim.                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Allure locally: pytest --alluredir=allure-results вҶ’ allure              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ generate/serve (Java; you have                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ JDK вҖ” fresh users get scoop install allure / npm i -g                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ allure-commandline in README); every suite                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ run ends by printing file:///вҖҰ/allure-report/index.html.                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Manual procedures (docs/manual-tests.md, copy-paste + expected result): в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ real Gmail SMTP send                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ (app password in .env), toast visual, TUI walkthrough, Jenkins UI run + в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Allure tab, GH Pages                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ report in browser.                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 7. CI/CD & Docker                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ GitHub Actions (.github/workflows/ci.yml), three jobs:                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - test (push/PR): setup-python 3.12 вҶ’ pip install -e .[dev] + ruff вҶ’    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ruff check +                                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ pytest -m smoke -q --alluredir=allure-results +                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ behave --tags=@smoke -f allure_behave.formatter:AllureFormatter -o      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ allure-results features                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ вҶ’ actions/upload-artifact@v4 (single merged results dir).               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - allure-pages (master only, needs: test, if: always()): download       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ results вҶ’                                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ simple-elf/allure-report-action@v1.9 (keeps history/trend) вҶ’            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ peaceiris/actions-gh-pages@v4.                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - sarif (permissions: security-events: write): install tool вҶ’ analyze   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sample_logs/... --export sarif --output findings.sarif --no-alerts ||   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ true (exit 1 = findings, expected) вҶ’                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v3 with category. SARIF URIs are      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ repo-relative                                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ (sample_logs/access.log) so findings annotate committed sample lines in в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Security вҶ’ Code                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ scanning (public repo = free).                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Jenkins (Jenkinsfile, native Windows agent): triggers { pollSCM('H/5 *  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ * * *') } (local                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Jenkins can't get webhooks without a tunnel), stages Setup (py -3.12 -m в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ venv + install) вҶ’                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Regression (pytest -q --alluredir=allure-results then                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ behave -f allure_behave.formatter:AllureFormatter -o allure-results     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ features вҖ” either failing                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ fails the stage), post { always { allure ... } } via the Allure Jenkins в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ plugin. Can it fail the build? Yes вҖ” pytest's nonzero exit fails the    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ bat step вҶ’ RED                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ build; junit-plugin UNSTABLE (yellow) is possible but recommendation:   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ fail hard вҖ” a regression                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ suite exists to block merges. Setup steps documented: Pipeline job вҶ’    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ SCM = repo, script path                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Jenkinsfile, install Allure plugin + Commandline tool, one manual run   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ for the screenshot.                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Docker: python:3.12-slim вҶ’ non-root appuser вҶ’ pip install . вҶ’           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ENTRYPOINT ["security-log-analysis-tool"], CMD ["--help"]. Usage:       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker run --rm -v "%CD%\sample_logs:/logs:ro" slat analyze             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ /logs/access.log /logs/auth.log.                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ .dockerignore: tests, .git, .claude, node_modules, session-logs,        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ allure-, .env.                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 8. 48h feasibility triage (~16h attention; parallel sessions absorb     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ wall-clock)                                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Verdict: the full scope fits, with ~2h of slack, if the cut list is     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ respected.                                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - MUST (assessment core, вүҲ7h): S1 + S2 + core README вҖ” parsers, all     в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ 9. Risks & mitigations                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ                                                                    в”Ӯ

вқҜ why does session 3 needs 2 to be completed?                                   

в—Ҹ Because session-3's job queue actually runs the analysis pipeline that
  session-2 builds вҖ” it's not just an abstract queue.

  Concretely: session-3's WorkerPool workers call pipeline/engine.py (the files
  вҶ’ events вҶ’ detectors вҶ’ correlation вҶ’ findings engine), which is a session-2 
  deliverable. And session-3's performance suite asserts on real results вҖ” the
  20-concurrent-jobs test checks each job's findings count, the throughput test
  streams a real log through the detectors. None of those assertions mean
  anything without session-2's engine and detection rules present. That's why
  its cold-start prompt says "verify session-2's pipeline/engine.py is merged
  into your base" before starting.

  So the dependency is genuine, not conservative padding.

  That said вҖ” it's the one dependency in the DAG you could break if you wanted
  more parallelism. The queue/worker-pool/registry machinery itself
  (backpressure, graceful shutdown, cancellation) is conceptually independent of
  what the workers execute. Session-3 could build against a stub engine(files) 
  -> findings and run in Wave 2 alongside session-2 and session-4, then do a
  small integration pass when session-2's real engine lands. The trade-off:
  you'd write a throwaway stub and defer the perf-test-on-real-findings
  assertions to that integration step, which adds a merge-time reconciliation
  and a bit of risk. I gated it on session-2 instead because the perf tests are
  more credible run against the real pipeline, and the wall-clock cost is low вҖ”
  session-3 is a 2вҖ“4h session that starts the moment session-2 signals done.

  Want me to decouple it (stub engine, move session-3 into Wave 2)? It's a
  one-line change to its blocked by plus a note in its prompt to build against
  the stub вҖ” I can do that in the plan and re-sync the manifest. Otherwise the
  current gating stands.

в—Ҹ No вҖ” firing session-7 now would run it against a repo that's basically empty.
  It's the final validation session: its whole job is to merge every session

  2вҖ“6 don't exist yet, there are no branches to merge, no detectors/queue/TUI/CI

  or, worse, "succeed" vacuously and fire the ALL-DONE toast telling you
  everything's validated when nothing was built.

  That's exactly what its gate prevents вҖ” it's blocked on all six sessions
  precisely so it can't start early. Its tab is sitting in the self-gating poll
  loop and will auto-submit the moment session-6 (the last of its blockers)
  signals .done. There's no reason to fire it by hand, and every reason not to.

  If your worry is "will session-7 actually start on its own?" вҖ” yes, the gate
  we verified in the dry run lists all six blockers, so it self-submits with no
  manual Enter once they're all done. If you want to watch that gating happen,
  orchestration-status.ps1 -PlanSlug 'logwarden' shows session-7 flipping from

  session-7's work sooner (say, a partial integration check after sessions 2вҖ“4

вҖ» recap: Building the security-log-analysis tool via 7 orchestrated sessions; sessions 1вҖ“4 and 6 are done, session-5 (TUI) is the last one running. Next: when it finishes, session-7 auto-fires the final validation and I'll summarize the report. (disable recaps in /config)

вқҜ Session 7 runs on fable, is there a reason for that?                          

в—Ҹ Yes вҖ” session-7 is the one place in the DAG where a top-tier, huge-context
  model actually earns its keep.

  Every other session is scoped to one module and reviews a single focused diff.
  Session-7 is the opposite: it's the integration/validation session, and its
  job is inherently whole-solution. It has to hold all six branches in context
  at once вҖ” merge them in dependency order, reconcile the cross-cutting seams
  where they meet (auth Г— pipeline, queue Г— TUI wiring via call_from_thread,
  exports Г— CI/SARIF, correlation Г— detectors), run the whole-solution E2E
  positive and negative, and consolidate seven reports into one coherent
  logwarden-final-report.md with an honest risk read. That's the kind of
  judgement that degrades when the model can't see the entire system at once or
  has to reason shallowly across it.

  That maps directly to the split-plan skill's own model guidance for the final
  validation session: Opus 4.8 by default, Fable 5 for architecture-heavy plans
  вҖ” "integration-level judgement across every branch; Fable's huge context suits
  plans with many cross-cutting sessions." This plan is squarely the
  architecture-heavy case (7 sessions, lots of cross-cutting concerns), so I
  picked Fable over Opus for the validation pass specifically.

  It's a deliberate premium spend on the one session that touches everything.
  Opus 4.8 would do a competent job too вҖ” if you'd rather not pay the Fable rate
  on it, it's a safe downgrade. But the implementation sessions are correctly
  on the cheaper tiers (Sonnet for the mechanical ones, Opus only where
  decisions propagate вҖ” foundations and the concurrency engine), so the cost is
  concentrated where the judgement is hardest. Session-7 hasn't started yet
  (still gated on session-5), so if you want to switch it to Opus I can adjust
  the manifest before it fires.

  Why not the very top: the first thing a reviewer needs is what this is вҖ” the
  tool, what it detects, the cross-source correlation hook. That orientation is
  what lets them judge the engineering, which is still the larger part of the
  grade. Leading with process before the product reads as burying the lede, and
  it can come across as compensating. Standard README shape (title вҶ’ what it is
  вҶ’ features вҶ’ run it) is also what a reviewer's eye expects, so making them
  scroll past a meta-section to find install/usage adds friction.

  Why you're still right to push on it: the brief explicitly says "We will 
  review how you collaborated with AI as part of our evaluation" вҖ” so AI
  collaboration is a first-class graded dimension, and right now it's the last
  section in the README, which under-sells it. Most candidates bury it;
  surfacing it deliberately is a differentiator.

  The move I'd make: keep the product intro leading, but add a short,
  high-visibility callout immediately after the intro paragraph / badges вҖ” one
  or two lines that point straight at the artifacts, e.g.:

  в–Һ Built with Claude Code. Planned and implemented as a multi-session agentic 
  в–Һ workflow вҖ” the full plan, per-session prompts, and verbatim transcripts are 
  в–Һ in session-logs/ and session-logs/plans/. See AI-assisted development.

  Then bump AI-assisted development up the Contents TOC (near the top of the
  list) so it's obviously present, while the detailed section stays where it is.
  That way the product still leads, but a reviewer skimming the first screen
  immediately sees you took the AI-collaboration requirement seriously and knows
  exactly where to look вҖ” without you performing it.

  If you want to go a step further, the callout is also the perfect place to
  name the approach in one clause ("7 scoped sessions, dependency-gated,
  parallel worktrees") вҖ” because the workflow itself is evidence of
  sophisticated AI collaboration, which is exactly what they're scoring.

  Want me to add the top callout and reorder the TOC entry? I'll fold it into
  the same pending end-of-session commit.
